      <article class="post-2609 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-1-minute-guide category-django category-frontend category-guides category-html-css category-js tag-collectstatic tag-static-files" id="post-2609">
       <figure class="entry-featured-image">
        <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/12/18/static-files-versioning-in-django/" rel="bookmark" title="Static Files Versioning in Django">
         <img alt="" class="attachment-nucleare-normal-post size-nucleare-normal-post wp-post-image" data-attachment-id="2620" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-caption="" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="Screenshot 2022-12-18 at 15.56.08" data-large-file="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.56.08.png?w=430" data-medium-file="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.56.08.png?w=300" data-orig-file="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.56.08.png" data-orig-size="430,91" data-permalink="https://djangokatya.com/2022/12/18/static-files-versioning-in-django/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15-56-08/" decoding="async" height="91" sizes="(max-width: 430px) 100vw, 430px" src="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.56.08.png?w=430" srcset="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.56.08.png 430w, https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.56.08.png?w=150 150w, https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.56.08.png?w=300 300w" width="430"/>
         <figcaption>
          <p>
           <i class="fa fa-file-text">
           </i>
          </p>
         </figcaption>
        </a>
       </figure>
       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title">
         <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/12/18/static-files-versioning-in-django/" rel="bookmark">
          Static Files Versioning in Django
         </a>
        </h1>
        <div class="entry-meta small-part">
         <span class="posted-on">
          <i class="fa fa-clock-o space-left-right">
          </i>
          <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/12/18/static-files-versioning-in-django/" rel="bookmark">
           <time class="entry-date published updated" datetime="2022-12-18T15:58:01+03:00">
            18.12.2022
           </time>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="byline">
          <i class="fa fa-user space-left-right">
          </i>
          <span class="author vcard">
           <a class="url fn n" href="https://djangokatya.com/author/katjadmin/">
            djangokatya
           </a>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="comments-link">
          <i class="fa fa-comments-o space-left-right">
          </i>
          <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/12/18/static-files-versioning-in-django/#comments">
           1 Comment
          </a>
         </span>
        </div>
        <!-- .entry-meta -->
       </header>
       <!-- .entry-header -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <h2 class="wp-block-heading">
         Installation
        </h2>
        <p>
         It is pretty easy in 2.2+, just add to your settings:
        </p>
        <pre class="wp-block-code"><code>STATICFILES_STORAGE = 'django.contrib.staticfiles.storage.ManifestStaticFilesStorage'</code></pre>
        <p>
         Don’t forget to set:
        </p>
        <pre class="wp-block-code"><code>DEBUG = False</code></pre>
        <p>
         And do
         <code>
          collectstatic
         </code>
         . This way Django will run over all of your files and search for them in your statics directory.
        </p>
        <h2 class="wp-block-heading">
         ValueError: the file &lt;file_path&gt; could not be found
        </h2>
        <p>
         Be careful with urls – they might work on the website, but it the storage module may not identify the paths correctly. This error occurs:
        </p>
        <pre class="wp-block-code"><code>ValueError: The file 'css/plugins/fonts/fontawesome-webfont.eot' could not be found with &lt;django.contrib.staticfiles.storage.ManifestStaticFilesStorage object at 0x12ae4e220&gt;.</code></pre>
        <p>
         Because it has a path like this
        </p>
        <pre class="wp-block-code"><code>fonts/fontawesome-webfont.eot</code></pre>
        <p>
         You need to make it relative:
        </p>
        <pre class="wp-block-code"><code>../../fonts/fontawesome-webfont.eot</code></pre>
        <h2 class="wp-block-heading">
         RuntimeError: Max post-process passes exceeded.
        </h2>
        <p>
         If you see an error like this:
        </p>
        <pre class="wp-block-code"><code>Post-processing 'All' failed!
RuntimeError: Max post-process passes exceeded.</code></pre>
        <p>
         Then check your
         <code>
          @import
         </code>
         statements – remove the commented once and try to find where the import is circular.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <h2 class="wp-block-heading">
         Conclusion
        </h2>
        <p>
         Versioning does not tolerate uncarefully made static files. You may spend a few hours removing rudimental imports, files, altering paths, removing urls to non-existent files. That’s totally normal.
        </p>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-content -->
       <footer class="entry-footer">
        <div class="entry-bottom small-part">
        </div>
       </footer>
       <!-- .entry-footer -->

         <img alt="" class="attachment-nucleare-normal-post size-nucleare-normal-post wp-post-image" data-attachment-id="2622" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-caption="" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="Screenshot 2022-12-18 at 15.59.16" data-large-file="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.59.16.png?w=809" data-medium-file="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.59.16.png?w=300" data-orig-file="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.59.16.png" data-orig-size="870,235" data-permalink="https://djangokatya.com/2022/12/01/celery-schedule-tasks-with-pauses-between-them/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15-59-16/" decoding="async" height="219" sizes="(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px" src="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.59.16.png?w=810" srcset="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.59.16.png?w=810 810w, https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.59.16.png?w=150 150w, https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.59.16.png?w=300 300w, https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.59.16.png?w=768 768w, https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/12/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-15.59.16.png 870w" width="810"/>
         <figcaption>
          <p>
           <i class="fa fa-file-text">
           </i>
          </p>
         </figcaption>
        </a>
       </figure>
       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title">
         <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/12/01/celery-schedule-tasks-with-pauses-between-them/" rel="bookmark">
          Celery – schedule tasks with pauses between them
         </a>
        </h1>
        <div class="entry-meta small-part">
         <span class="posted-on">
          <i class="fa fa-clock-o space-left-right">
          </i>
          <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/12/01/celery-schedule-tasks-with-pauses-between-them/" rel="bookmark">
           <time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-12-01T20:04:01+03:00">
            01.12.2022
           </time>
           <time class="updated" datetime="2022-12-18T16:01:45+03:00">
            18.12.2022
           </time>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="byline">
          <i class="fa fa-user space-left-right">
          </i>
          <span class="author vcard">
           <a class="url fn n" href="https://djangokatya.com/author/katjadmin/">
            djangokatya
           </a>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="comments-link">
          <i class="fa fa-comments-o space-left-right">
          </i>
          <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/12/01/celery-schedule-tasks-with-pauses-between-them/#respond">
           Leave a comment
          </a>
         </span>
        </div>
        <!-- .entry-meta -->
       </header>
       <!-- .entry-header -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <p>
         I needed to schedule 10 tasks that have these conditions
        </p>
        <ol>
         <li>
          A time gap between tasks is fixed (but varies)
         </li>
         <li>
          No need to pass results of one task to another
         </li>
         <li>
          Need to read a database in every task (important: at the moment of the execution)
         </li>
        </ol>
        <p>
         I tried a few options, and this one worked
        </p>
        <pre class="wp-block-code"><code> ret = chain(task1.si(args).set(countdown=30*1), ..., task10.si(args).set(countdown=30*10)).apply_sync()</code></pre>
        <p>
         Important note – the signature here is not .s() but .si() this way you don’t pass the result of task1 to task2. You set the countdown with set() and not inside the apply_sync().
        </p>
        <p>
         It is simple but it took me some time to figure out.
        </p>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-content -->
       <footer class="entry-footer">
        <div class="entry-bottom small-part">
        </div>
       </footer>
       <!-- .entry-footer -->
      </article>

      <article class="post-2594 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-django category-notes" id="post-2594">
       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title">
         <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/11/06/dont-use-on_deletemodels-cascade-carelessly/" rel="bookmark">
          Don’t use on_delete=models.CASCADE carelessly
         </a>
        </h1>
        <div class="entry-meta small-part">
         <span class="posted-on">
          <i class="fa fa-clock-o space-left-right">
          </i>
          <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/11/06/dont-use-on_deletemodels-cascade-carelessly/" rel="bookmark">
           <time class="entry-date published updated" datetime="2022-11-06T20:37:17+03:00">
            06.11.2022
           </time>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="byline">
          <i class="fa fa-user space-left-right">
          </i>
          <span class="author vcard">
           <a class="url fn n" href="https://djangokatya.com/author/katjadmin/">
            djangokatya
           </a>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="comments-link">
          <i class="fa fa-comments-o space-left-right">
          </i>
          <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/11/06/dont-use-on_deletemodels-cascade-carelessly/#comments">
           1 Comment
          </a>
         </span>
        </div>
        <!-- .entry-meta -->
       </header>
       <!-- .entry-header -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <p>
         Don’t every use it inside a model that is not intended to be deleted depending on the relation (ForeignKeyField or OneToOneField) being dropped or not.
        </p>
        <p>
         That’s it, that’s the note.
        </p>
       </div>

      <article class="post-2548 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-django category-frontend category-js category-notes" id="post-2548">
       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title">
         <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/08/27/a-short-note-about-js/" rel="bookmark">
          A short note about JS
         </a>
        </h1>
        <div class="entry-meta small-part">
         <span class="posted-on">
          <i class="fa fa-clock-o space-left-right">
          </i>
          <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/08/27/a-short-note-about-js/" rel="bookmark">
           <time class="entry-date published updated" datetime="2022-08-27T00:46:40+03:00">
            27.08.2022
           </time>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="byline">
          <i class="fa fa-user space-left-right">
          </i>
          <span class="author vcard">
           <a class="url fn n" href="https://djangokatya.com/author/katjadmin/">
            djangokatya
           </a>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="comments-link">
          <i class="fa fa-comments-o space-left-right">
          </i>
          <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/08/27/a-short-note-about-js/#respond">
           Leave a comment
          </a>
         </span>
        </div>
        <!-- .entry-meta -->
       </header>
       <!-- .entry-header -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <p>

        </p>
        <p>
         Just a short note to tell you about the fun I’ve having 😉
        </p>

         <img alt="" class="attachment-nucleare-normal-post size-nucleare-normal-post wp-post-image" data-attachment-id="2623" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-caption="" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="Screenshot 2022-12-18 at 16.03.06" data-large-file="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/08/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.03.06.png?w=809" data-medium-file="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/08/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.03.06.png?w=300" data-orig-file="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/08/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.03.06.png" data-orig-size="897,227" data-permalink="https://djangokatya.com/2022/08/18/macos-m1-m1-pro-ffmpeg-with-mp3-support-and-opencv/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16-03-06/" decoding="async" height="205" loading="lazy" sizes="(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px" src="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/08/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.03.06.png?w=810" srcset="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/08/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.03.06.png?w=810 810w, https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/08/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.03.06.png?w=150 150w, https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/08/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.03.06.png?w=300 300w, https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/08/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.03.06.png?w=768 768w, https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/08/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.03.06.png 897w" width="810"/>

       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title">
         <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/08/18/macos-m1-m1-pro-ffmpeg-with-mp3-support-and-opencv/" rel="bookmark">
          macOS (M1/M1 Pro) – ffmpeg with mp3 support and OpenCV
         </a>
        </h1>
        <div class="entry-meta small-part">
         <span class="posted-on">
          <i class="fa fa-clock-o space-left-right">
          </i>
          <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/08/18/macos-m1-m1-pro-ffmpeg-with-mp3-support-and-opencv/" rel="bookmark">
           <time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-08-18T18:58:07+03:00">
            18.08.2022
           </time>
           <time class="updated" datetime="2022-12-18T16:03:47+03:00">
            18.12.2022
           </time>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="byline">
          <i class="fa fa-user space-left-right">
          </i>
          <span class="author vcard">
           <a class="url fn n" href="https://djangokatya.com/author/katjadmin/">
            djangokatya
           </a>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="comments-link">
          <i class="fa fa-comments-o space-left-right">
          </i>
          <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/08/18/macos-m1-m1-pro-ffmpeg-with-mp3-support-and-opencv/#respond">
           Leave a comment
          </a>
         </span>
        </div>
        <!-- .entry-meta -->
       </header>
       <!-- .entry-header -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <p>
         This is not funny – I spent a few evening fixing and fixing and fixing. Now ./configure then make and sudo make, but where is binary? Why is it not is
         <strong>
          /usr/bin/
         </strong>
         OR
         <strong>
          /usr/local/bin/
         </strong>
         ? Oh you do
         <strong>
          brew install opencv
         </strong>
         – but it does not work in terminal? Amazing. I was THIS close to wiping mac os and installing Linux on my macbook guys, THIS CLOSE.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Anyhow it is simple if you do the right thing.
        </p>
        <h2 class="wp-block-heading">
         ffmpeg with mp3 support
        </h2>
        <pre class="wp-block-code"><code>brew uninstall lame —force
brew uninstall homebrew-ffmpeg/ffmpeg/ffmpeg
brew install homebrew-ffmpeg/ffmpeg/ffmpeg —with-fdk-aac
</code></pre>
        <h2 class="wp-block-heading">
         In your virtualenv
        </h2>
        <pre class="wp-block-code"><code>pip uninstall ffmpeg
pip uninstall ffmpeg-python
pip install ffmpeg-python</code></pre>
        <p>
         And then install OpenCV (it is now working with pip):
        </p>
        <pre class="wp-block-code"><code>pip install opencv-python</code></pre>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-content -->
       <footer class="entry-footer">
        <div class="entry-bottom small-part">
        </div>
       </footer>

      <article class="post-2523 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-django tag-djangoadmin tag-optimization" id="post-2523">
       <figure class="entry-featured-image">
        <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/04/17/how-to-speed-up-django-admin-foreignkey-and-manytomanyfield/" rel="bookmark" title="How to speed up Django Admin: Foreignkey and ManyToManyField">
         <img alt="" class="attachment-nucleare-normal-post size-nucleare-normal-post wp-post-image" data-attachment-id="2625" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-caption="" data-image-description="" data-image-meta='{"aperture":"0","credit":"","camera":"","caption":"","created_timestamp":"0","copyright":"","focal_length":"0","iso":"0","shutter_speed":"0","title":"","orientation":"0"}' data-image-title="Screenshot 2022-12-18 at 16.07.04" data-large-file="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/04/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.07.04.png?w=809" data-medium-file="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/04/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.07.04.png?w=300" data-orig-file="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/04/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.07.04.png" data-orig-size="867,233" data-permalink="https://djangokatya.com/2022/04/17/how-to-speed-up-django-admin-foreignkey-and-manytomanyfield/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16-07-04/" decoding="async" height="218" loading="lazy" sizes="(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px" src="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/04/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.07.04.png?w=810" srcset="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/04/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.07.04.png?w=810 810w, https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/04/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.07.04.png?w=150 150w, https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/04/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.07.04.png?w=300 300w, https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/04/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.07.04.png?w=768 768w, https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/04/screenshot-2022-12-18-at-16.07.04.png 867w" width="810"/>
         <figcaption>
          <p>
           <i class="fa fa-file-text">
           </i>
          </p>
         </figcaption>
        </a>
       </figure>
       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title">
         <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/04/17/how-to-speed-up-django-admin-foreignkey-and-manytomanyfield/" rel="bookmark">
          How to speed up Django Admin: Foreignkey and ManyToManyField
         </a>
        </h1>
        <div class="entry-meta small-part">
         <span class="posted-on">
          <i class="fa fa-clock-o space-left-right">
          </i>
          <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/04/17/how-to-speed-up-django-admin-foreignkey-and-manytomanyfield/" rel="bookmark">
           <time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-04-17T19:05:09+03:00">
            17.04.2022
           </time>
           <time class="updated" datetime="2022-12-18T16:08:20+03:00">
            18.12.2022
           </time>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="byline">
          <i class="fa fa-user space-left-right">
          </i>
          <span class="author vcard">
           <a class="url fn n" href="https://djangokatya.com/author/katjadmin/">
            djangokatya
           </a>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="comments-link">
          <i class="fa fa-comments-o space-left-right">
          </i>
          <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/04/17/how-to-speed-up-django-admin-foreignkey-and-manytomanyfield/#respond">
           Leave a comment
          </a>
         </span>
        </div>
        <!-- .entry-meta -->
       </header>
       <!-- .entry-header -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <p>
         If you have a Foreignkey or ManyToManyField in your admin form, but you don’t need to change it in any way, replace it with a label. Say, you have a model:
        </p>
        <pre class="wp-block-code"><code>class Student(models.Model):
    ...
    class_obj = models.ForeignKey('Class', on_delete=models.CASCADE)</code></pre>
        <p>
         And in your Django Admin you want to have thic field:
        </p>
        <pre class="wp-block-code"><code>@admin.register(Student)
class StudentAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    fields = ('class_obj',)</code></pre>
        <p>
         There is no problem if you have, say, 10-100 Class instances, but if you have thousands of them – the interface would take a lot of time to load.
        </p>
        <p>
         Instead of that, make a label property and replace the original field with it.
        </p>
        <pre class="wp-block-code"><code>class Student(models.Model):
    ...
    class_obj = models.ForeignKey('Class', on_delete=models.CASCADE)

<strong><mark class="has-inline-color" style="background-color:#8ed1fc">    @property
    def class_obj_str(self):
        return self.class.name</mark></strong></code></pre>
        <p>
         And then in the ModelAdmin:
        </p>
        <pre class="wp-block-code"><code>@admin.register(Student)
class StudentAdmin(admin.ModelAdmin):
    <strong><mark class="has-inline-color has-black-color" style="background-color:#8ed1fc">readonly_fields = ('class_str',)</mark></strong>
    fields = ('class_obj<strong><mark class="has-inline-color" style="background-color:#8ed1fc">_str</mark></strong>',)</code></pre>
        <p>
        </p>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-content -->
       <footer class="entry-footer">
        <div class="entry-bottom small-part">
        </div>
       </footer>
       <!-- .entry-footer -->
      </article>

      <article class="post-2490 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-python" id="post-2490">
       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title">
         <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/02/18/gitpython-diff-between-two-branches/" rel="bookmark">
          GitPython –  Diff between two branches
         </a>
        </h1>
        <div class="entry-meta small-part">
         <span class="posted-on">
          <i class="fa fa-clock-o space-left-right">
          </i>
          <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/02/18/gitpython-diff-between-two-branches/" rel="bookmark">
           <time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-02-18T14:28:39+03:00">
            18.02.2022
           </time>
           <time class="updated" datetime="2022-02-18T14:30:02+03:00">
            18.02.2022
           </time>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="byline">
          <i class="fa fa-user space-left-right">
          </i>
          <span class="author vcard">
           <a class="url fn n" href="https://djangokatya.com/author/katjadmin/">
            djangokatya
           </a>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="comments-link">
          <i class="fa fa-comments-o space-left-right">
          </i>
          <a href="https://djangokatya.com/2022/02/18/gitpython-diff-between-two-branches/#respond">
           Leave a comment
          </a>
         </span>
        </div>
        <!-- .entry-meta -->
       </header>
       <!-- .entry-header -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <div class="wpcom-reblog-snapshot">
         <div class="reblogger-note">
          <div class="reblogger-note-content">
           <blockquote>
            <p>
             <!-- wp:paragraph -->
            </p>
            <p>
             My dear brother started his own blog on Airflow, Python, PostgreSQL and Javascript!!!
            </p>
            <p>
             <!-- /wp:paragraph -->
            </p>
            <p>
             <!-- wp:paragraph -->
            </p>
            <p>
             Congrats, Ilia!
            </p>
            <p>
             <!-- /wp:paragraph -->
            </p>
           </blockquote>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="reblog-post">
          <p class="reblog-from">
           <img alt="" class="avatar avatar-32" height="32" loading="lazy" src="https://1.gravatar.com/avatar/1aeb581cf2ebf1e7acc6ff8fcdffa7e952ad0a43c890a4af6703dc85a1dd1acb?s=32&amp;d=retro&amp;r=G" width="32"/>
           <a href="https://iliasjavascriptjourney.wordpress.com/2022/02/16/gitpython-diff-between-two-branches/">
            Ilia's Airflow, Python, PostgreSQL, Javascript Journey
           </a>
          </p>
          <div class="reblogged-content">
           <p>
           </p>
           <h2>
            Code:
           </h2>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <pre class="wp-block-code has-background" style="background-color:#e9e9e9"><code>import os
from pathlib import Path 
from git import Repo

# path to repo folder
path = Path(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))

# repo variable
repo = Repo(path)

# Your last commit of the current branch
commit_feature = repo.head.commit.tree

# Your last commit of the dev branch
commit_origin_dev = repo.commit("origin/dev")
new_files = []
deleted_files = []
modified_files = []

# Comparing 
diff_index = commit_origin_dev.diff(commit_feature)

# Collection all new files
for file in diff_index.iter_change_type('A'):
    new_files.append(file)

# Collection all deleted files
for file in diff_index.iter_change_type('D'):
    deleted_files.append(file)

# Collection all modified files
for file in diff_index.iter_change_type('M'):
    modified_files.append(file)

</code></pre>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <h2>
            Analyze:
           </h2>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            Let’s imagine the situation:
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <figure class="wp-block-image size-large">
            <img class="wp-image-44" src="https://djangokatya.files.wordpress.com/2022/02/image-2.png"/>
            <figcaption>
             You are before code review and you need to
             <strong>
              get all changes between feature and develop
             </strong>
             with GitPython.
             <br/>
             First you need to get last commits from two branches:
            </figcaption>
           </figure>
           <p>
           </p>
           <pre class="wp-block-code has-cyan-bluish-gray-background-color has-background"><code># Your last commit of the current branch
commit_dev = repo.head.commit.tree

# Your last commit of the dev branch
commit_origin_dev = repo.commit("origin/dev")</code></pre>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <p>
            Then get your changes:
           </p>
          </div>
          <p class="reblog-source">
           <a href="https://iliasjavascriptjourney.wordpress.com/2022/02/16/gitpython-diff-between-two-branches/">
            View original post
           </a>
           <span class="more-words">
            81 more words
           </span>
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-content -->
       <footer class="entry-footer">
        <div class="entry-bottom small-part">
        </div>
       </footer>
